building_gold_mine1x = {
    scope = country
        effect = {
            every_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                has_decree = decree_my_dear_sakuya
            }

                create_building = {
                    building = building_gold_mine
                    level = 1
            }
        }  
    }
}

	effect = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_decree = decree_my_dear_sakuya
			}
			create_building = {
				building = building_logging_camp
				level = 300
			}
		}
	}
}
